<rating>3<//rating>< Review>
It wasn't all that long ago that frozen yogurt was THE thing to get, but no longer is that the case.  Still, it's nice to stop in a get a cup of your favorite flavors on a warm day, after a movie or show, or anytime you are looking for a sweet dessert that doesn't feel entirely decadent (it's yogurt, right?!?).  There is seating outdoors and in, and there are extra chairs in the corner in case you come with a crowd.  Toppings are offered at the end, and everything is weighed to determine the cost.</Review>
